2b1(kha): bag chags kun/ zla ba nya nas stong bar bzhin/ ma yang rang zhi rang sal grol/ grol ba nyid la sgom mi dgos zhes bya ste/ gsang ba dgu 'phar gyi rtsa tshig gi le'u ste dang po'o//

3a1(kha): @/ brtsigs can/ 'jigs byed dregs pa'i ka gdang dbyam/ gyur tig cig dang bcas pa la/ sa bdag rigs pa tshe 'brul gdan/ dpag du med pa bdag gis sgom/
